British Mediterranean Fleet Begins to Return to Original Defense; Believes Germany More Important Than Italy; Signs of Improved Relations Between Britain and Italy; France Announces Mutual Assistance Measures Invalid 31

(London) The Admiralty has begun today to withdraw the main fleet stationed in the Mediterranean. However, the Mediterranean fleet will be stronger than before the Italian-Abyssinian War. Several of the withdrawing ships will head to the Far East. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) The government suddenly decided to redeploy the main fleet currently stationed in Gibraltar. Political figures explained that recent rumors suggested that if the British main fleet did not return to its original defense and the mutual assistance agreements of the Mediterranean countries were not revoked, Italy would refuse to participate in the Montreux Conference and future Locarno Conference. The government feared that Italy might issue a formal note to Britain at any moment, stating this intention. Therefore, it was decided to withdraw the fleet automatically as a preemptive measure. It was also stated that the government now believes that the dangers that Germany might pose are more significant than the Italian issue. It is imperative to redeploy the fleet to the North Sea for defense, which also provides clear evidence of this. (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

(Rome) Government officials here were very pleased to hear that the British government had decided to redeploy the main fleet currently stationed in the Mediterranean back to its original defense. They stated that to clarify the international situation, all sanction-related measures should be revoked first. Italy has long held this view and has never changed. Officials are still silent about the future trend of Italian foreign policy and refuse to comment on whether Italy will participate in the Montreux Conference and future Locarno Conference. They only stated that they would clarify after the British fleet has indeed withdrawn. Some optimists said that after the British main fleet is redeployed to its original defense, the Italian troops stationed in Libya, North Africa, will soon be recalled to Italy. (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

(London) Regarding the impending redeployment of the fleet stationed in the Mediterranean, official sources recently announced that the Mediterranean countries (excluding Britain and Italy) had previously signed a mutual assistance agreement based on Section 3 of Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant. This agreement will not be affected in any way by the withdrawal of British warships. (Note: This section states that "The Members of the League agree that, when financial or economic measures are taken in accordance with this Article, they will mutually support one to another in order to minimise the loss and inconvenience resulting therefrom, and that they will mutually support one another in resisting any special measures aimed at one of their number by the covenant-breaking State, and that they will take the necessary steps to afford passage through their territory to the forces of any of the Members of the League which are co-operating to protect the covenants of the League.") (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

Britain Increases Naval Strength in the Far East 32

Mediterranean Fleet Redeployed to China

(London) The British warships that hastily sailed from the Far East to the Mediterranean when the Italian-Abyssinian War broke out have now been relieved of their special duties and will soon sail back to their original defense in China. This action follows the British government's decision to reduce the strength of the British Mediterranean Fleet to normal levels. It is reported that the original defense in China will maintain full naval strength and may even be slightly increased. Two escape-ocean ships and four submarines will return to the Far East within days. Four D-class destroyers will sail from Aden to the Far East. The cruiser "Cumberland," formerly belonging to the British fleet in China, has been extensively refurbished at a cost of £561,000. Its appearance has undergone significant modifications. It will sail to China again in September to replace the cruiser Cornwall, which will arrive here on July 14. The new Australian cruiser Sydney, after being launched in Britain, sailed to the Mediterranean due to the emergency there. It will now sail to Australia, where Australians will see it for the first time. The accelerated progress of British defense programs will have a steadying effect on the European continent. As for its funding, the budget has stipulated an additional £25,600,000 for defense, so the new bill only exceeds the expected amount by £4,000,000. All funds will be used domestically, and most of it will return to the treasury. (Reuters, 10th)

(London) The government has decided to redeploy the warships stationed in the Mediterranean to their original defense. The names of these warships and their fleet affiliations are listed below:

(A) Belonging to the Main Fleet stationed in Gibraltar: Battleships "Nelson" and "Rodney" (both 34,000 tons), three 7,000-ton cruisers: "Orion," "Leander," and "Neptune," aircraft carrier "Furious," nine 2,000-ton destroyers: "Campbell," "Comet," "Crescent," "Bedouin," "Wessex," "Codrington," "Vega," "Gallant," nine 1,500-ton destroyers: "Falknor," "Fearless," "Fortune," "Fame," "Forester," "Firedrake," "Foxhound," "Foresight," "Fury," nine submarines: "Titian," "Seawolf," "Seal," "Shark," "Swordfish," "Oberon," "L23," "L26," "L27."

(B) Belonging to the West Indies Fleet: Two cruisers: "Exeter," 8,400 tons, "Ajax," 6,900 tons.

(C) Belonging to the China Fleet: 10,000-ton cruiser "Berwick," mine-laying ship "Adventure," 8,000 tons, 15th Destroyer Division (currently stationed in Aden) and four submarines: "Osiris," "Oswald," "Pandora," "Proteus."

(D) Belonging to the Australian Fleet: 7,000-ton cruiser "Sydney."

(E) Belonging to the New Zealand Fleet: 7,000-ton cruiser "Achilles." (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

France Automatically Revokes Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Obligations 33

Officially Notifies British and Italian Governments

(Paris) The government has formally notified the British and Italian governments, stating that the French government believes that after the League of Nations General Assembly recently resolved to lift sanctions against Italy, the various mutual assistance measures previously agreed upon by Britain and France under Section 3 of Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant have been automatically cancelled. In addition, observers here expressed satisfaction with the British main fleet's decision to redeploy from the Mediterranean back to its original defense. (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

(Paris) The mutual assistance measures previously agreed upon by Britain and France have been declared invalid by the French government. The details are as follows: Earlier this week, the Italian government notified the French cabinet that since the League of Nations General Assembly had announced the lifting of sanctions, the mutual assistance measures previously agreed upon by Britain and France in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant would be regarded as an act of opposition by the Italian government if they were still maintained. The French authorities replied that the above-mentioned mutual assistance measures had been decided to be revoked several weeks ago. Until yesterday, it was decided to notify the British government of the exchange of documents between the two parties. (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

(London) Well-informed sources recently announced that after France declared the mutual assistance measures between Britain and France regarding the Mediterranean invalid yesterday, the counselor of the Turkish Embassy visited officials in the Foreign Office this morning to inquire about the matter. The official replied that whether the mutual assistance measures between Britain and France were invalid or not, the mutual assistance measures previously established by the Balkan countries would continue to be effective. Political figures explained that Britain now wants to resolve the Mediterranean issue completely and involve Italy, so that the original mutual assistance measures of Britain and France can become a general convention. (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

Disagreement on Key Issues; Montreux Conference Reaches Impasse 34

Britain Guarantees Not to Hinder Regional Mutual Assistance Conventions; Resolutely Opposes Black Sea Fleet Sailing into Mediterranean; Representatives Return Home for Instructions; General Assembly to Reconvene on Monday

Montreux The Montreux Conference has again reached an impasse due to the failure to resolve several important issues. (The conference was adjourned once last month.) Work can only continue after the governments of the relevant countries have stated their positions. It has been decided to hold a plenary session next Monday (the 13th). Many representatives from the relevant countries have now returned home for instructions. Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu left for home yesterday. British representative Lytton also returned to London yesterday morning and will return here next Monday. French Chief Delegate Poncet held talks with Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov and British Chief Delegate Lord Stanley separately and is scheduled to return home this afternoon. During the meeting with Stanley, Poncet immediately gave a guarantee that Britain has no intention of hindering the right of signatory countries to communicate with each other regarding the various constraints of all regional conventions (such as the Balkan Entente, the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty) that are to be added to the treaty for the purpose of maintaining a peaceful situation, whether in the Near East or other places. What Britain firmly insists on is that the Soviet Black Sea Fleet should not be allowed to freely enter the Mediterranean to unite with the Baltic Sea Fleet. Poncet expressed satisfaction with this guarantee, believing that Article 23 of the British draft (i.e., the one concerning regional conventions) can be revised to create a compromise. In addition, Britain and France have reached a consensus on the following two issues: The Straits Commission should continue to exist. Although Turkey has expressed opposition, the general nature of the agreement will not be hindered as a result. Regarding the issue of airplanes flying over the Straits, although Turkey has agreed to propose amendments to allow airplanes of all countries to pass through the Straits, they will not be allowed to fly over fortified areas. However, this statement is considered empty. It will require continued efforts from the representatives of the relevant countries to hope for a compromise. The points on which the relevant countries have mutually agreed are being drafted into a convention by the legal experts of each country, so that they can be completed before the plenary session next Monday. In addition, regarding Italy's participation in the conference, the delegations of the relevant countries expressed pessimism, believing that although Britain will withdraw the main fleet from the Mediterranean back to its original defense and France has decided to cancel the mutual assistance measures, Italy still has no hope of sending representatives to attend. (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

Montreux Observers believe that the situation at the Montreux Conference shows that the relevant countries still have disagreements on two issues: The Soviet Union's demand that its fleet should have the right to freely pass through the Straits, whether in wartime or peacetime. The Soviet Union's amendment to Article 16 of the British proposal (which advocates that the Black Sea should remain open in wartime), demanding that the Black Sea be closed in wartime, but that the fleets of all countries should be allowed to pass through freely if they are fulfilling the obligations stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant or regional conventions to deal with aggressor countries. Regarding the first issue, the British delegation has requested instructions from its government and will likely answer with "difficult to comply," because if the Soviet fleet stationed in the Black Sea is allowed to freely pass through the Straits to unite with the Baltic Sea Fleet, Germany would be unhappy, and the provisions of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement would also be hindered. Regarding the second issue, well-informed sources recently announced that Britain will likely agree, but according to the opinions of its experts, it must be accompanied by a condition: if Turkey is attacked for fulfilling regional conventions, Britain does not have to provide assistance and can stay out of it in accordance with the provisions of Section 7 of Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. (Note: This section states that "If the report by the Council is not unanimously agreed to by the members thereof, other than the Representatives of one or more of the parties to the dispute, the Members of the League reserve to themselves the right to take such action as they shall consider necessary for the maintenance of right and justice.") (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

Four Main Difficulties

Montreux Observers here recently stated that the difficulties currently encountered at the Montreux Conference can ultimately be resolved. The main difficulties are four: The Soviet Union firmly insists that various warships, even those of medium tonnage, should not be allowed to pass through the Straits. The warships of so-called medium tonnage clearly refer to the German pocket battleships of 10,000 tons. The Soviet Union demands that its navy, when sailing from the Black Sea into the Mediterranean, should have complete freedom without restrictions. The Soviet Union advocates that the Black Sea should be closed in wartime, and that no warships should be allowed to pass through, except for those fulfilling mutual assistance obligations. The Soviet Union demands that its warships should have the right to freely pass through the Straits when implementing regional agreements, such as the Balkan Entente or the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty. Among these, the last one is the most complex, and France has already supported it. (Havas Dispatch, 9th)

Romanian Representative Accuses British Policy of Contradiction

Montreux Today, when the Dardanelles Straits Conference considered the Russian representative's amendments to the British draft, a dispute arose between the British delegation and Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu. The Soviet amendments stated that the convention should not infringe upon the rights and obligations of the contracting countries as members of the League of Nations and should maintain the freedom of warships engaged in auxiliary defense against aggressors, either under the League Covenant or under supplementary treaties concluded within the League framework, to pass through the Straits. When the British representative explained his views, Titulescu was not present, but after arriving, he demanded a restatement of Britain's position. He then accused the British delegation, saying, "You advocate one policy in Geneva, and another policy here. You are trying to undermine mutual assistance and regional agreements." British Under-Secretary of State Cadogan replied that, out of courtesy, he intended to explain Britain's views, but that Titulescu's accusations were unfounded. Titulescu then rose again and said, "This is not a matter of courtesy. You are endangering the agreements between my country and France and the Balkan countries." After the meeting, Titulescu immediately took a train back to his country, as there seemed to be a dispute within the Romanian cabinet. The British delegation did not reject the Soviet proposal, but the difficulties that the conference will cause, this proposal will certainly be supported by France and the Balkan countries. The next plenary meeting is scheduled to be held next Monday. (Reuters, 9th)

Turkey Should Have Full Authority Over the Straits

Istanbul, Turkey Nati, a member of parliament, recently made a statement to the semi-official newspaper "Cumhuriyet" regarding the Straits issue, saying that the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits should be under the full authority of Turkey, without any restrictions. Regarding this case, Turkey's attitude is very moderate. Those who accuse it of closing its doors and not engaging in trade with the civilized world are not justified. Any country that wants to obtain the right of free passage through the Straits, Turkey should have the means to deal with it. Therefore, the Straits issue will no longer be a pending case. As for which countries the Straits should be closed to and which countries they should be open to, Turkey also knows how to plan. (Havas Dispatch, 10th)

In short, the French military industry has always supplied weapons to foreign countries and has also purchased foreign patent certificates to manufacture new types of equipment. It is especially necessary to adopt reciprocal measures for friendly countries. Côte refused to explain what military or technical items the Soviet Union had supplied to France. He also criticized Grillis's motion, saying that it could cause foreign countries to misunderstand and believe that France and Russia had concluded a secret treaty in addition to the mutual assistance treaty. In fact, "France and Russia have not concluded a military alliance treaty." The House of Representatives finally passed a vote of confidence in the government by a vote of 403 to 162. The Turmoil in Spain (Part 1) 39

— Authored by Louis Fisher, translated by Bin Fu

Spain clearly needs to find a way to alleviate her poverty and backwardness. Farmers and urban workers are demanding better living conditions. When the reactionary right-wingers were in power, they only responded to these demands with terror; thus, most Spaniards realized that the reactionaries no longer had the strength or the qualification to continue ruling the country.

The reactionary right-wing includes the large landowners, the Church, imperialists, and a few large industrialists. They are declining, shrinking, and disorganized. Their main hope at present is to obtain the assistance of the army and the Civil Guard to carry out a violent coup d'état. This kind of conspiracy is enough to show their loss of power. As a result, the left has obtained an unprecedented opportunity. On February 6, 1936, the United Front of the radicals finally achieved the final victory. Although the Communist Party refused to assume administrative responsibility, it finally gave support and maintenance to the minority cabinet of the left-wing bourgeois Republicans under the leadership of Azaña.

Manuel Azaña is an interesting figure in an interesting environment. Spain really needs a revolution to transform her national economy. Azaña hoped to achieve this revolution through evolution or democratic methods. Although socialists and communists watched with suspicion, they did not withdraw their support. The reasons for this were twofold: the overthrow of Azaña might lead to the restoration of right-wing rule, and they believed that Azaña's actions were paving the way for them. Azaña did not think so. He did not want to be Kerensky. He wanted to create a new and special category for Spain that neither coincided with Fascism or Bolshevism, nor was the same as the established forms of capitalism. He once said to me: "I want an extremely left-wing republic with some socialist reforms."

Although Azaña was not a socialist, he repeatedly mentioned to me "socialist reforms," "collective agriculture," and "the nationalization of land without compensation." The fact is that many who usually strongly oppose socialists believe that socialism is inevitable in Spain. The country must have a progressive class to lead and rule. In Western European countries, the bourgeoisie assumed this task, benefiting themselves, the country, and even the masses to some extent. But Spain has never developed into a bourgeoisie. This may be the reason for her decline. Now it is too late to create a Spanish bourgeoisie; the working and peasant masses are rising to seize power, to extricate themselves from misery, and to make Spain a modern and prosperous country.

Among Spain's 23,000,000 residents, 80% live in rural areas. If you add the official class and the urban intellectual class, the remaining industrial bourgeoisie is very limited. There is hardly a middle class. Under the empire, the Church was merely a system to help win over the people in darkness and ignorance. The people do not truly believe in religion; they resent the Church because it is the de facto spokesperson for their oppressors. All of this is very similar to the situation in Russia before 1917, and the conditions are also compatible with the same future development.

Not many days ago, I ran to the village of Pueblo del Rio, only thirty minutes by electric train from Seville. I had not been there for less than two years. The farmers immediately recognized me. I ran to the thatched mud huts. It was raining, and puddles had formed on the ground. The people were all poor and tattered; they had always suffered a lot, and according to their reports, "good or bad, nothing has changed." They were all vehemently opposed to the Church, and none of their children had been baptized. "The Church is only for the superstitious and the imperialists," one person said.

These farmers have nothing of their own—except for a few broken chairs, a table not good for eating, and a few crude benches used as beds. They work as day laborers for the large landowners, with a minimum wage of five "Peseta" (Spanish currency). They only have an average of three months of work per year. "Recently, under the compulsion of the government, there is finally more work, but the landlords do not pay wages. They live in Seville and Madrid, but there is no money." These people are so threatened by life that they dare not curse the wealthy. I have seen the Bedouin in the East. (Arabs who live in the Sahara and live a very hard life. - Translator) The lives of these Spaniards are really no better than theirs. There are tens of thousands of people living like this in Spain, living in caves and eating grass roots and bark.

This is naturally the lowest and most inferior dregs of humanity. But the "Yunteros," who have a pair of mules but no land, even those with one or two hectares of land, do not live comfortably. I have talked to twenty of these people. They are all malnourished. Their thirty-five-year-old women look about fifty years old. I asked a mother with four children why she had so many children. She replied: "They came, I would rather have none." In Caceres, the largest province in Spain, 61.6% of the population is illiterate. Other provinces are its sharp enemies. All of this is a death sentence for the ruling class.

Page 10

U.S. Army Major General Condemns Japanese, German, and Italian Ambitions 42

U.S. Involvement in War Is Almost Inevitable

Raphael, a Major General of the U.S. Army Reserve, stated in a speech at Virginia University today that Japan, Germany, and Italy are actively expanding their armaments in preparation for becoming international bandits. All three countries are industrial nations that, due to economic pressure from other countries, are eager to find supplies of raw materials and markets for selling goods. Therefore, the tariff barriers and import quotas of most countries are forcing the three countries to fight. The United States is facing two crises: one is that some militaristic countries intend to seize U.S. territory by force, and the other is that the United States will not be able to avoid being drawn into the vortex of the European war. Germany Respects Austrian Status Quo, Central European Bloc Revived

(Paris) Madame Tabouis, a diplomatic correspondent for the "L'Œuvre" newspaper, recently commented on the compromise reached between Germany and Italy, stating that the two countries seem to have agreed on a plan, the main points of which are no more than two: 1. To demand the amendment of the Covenant of the League of Nations and to delete the sanctions clauses. 2. Regarding the colonial demands, she said, "I have received news from Austrian officialdom that the country is currently in negotiations with Germany, hoping to establish an agreement in politics and economics. This is at the instigation of Italy. At the same time, Italy has also given assurances to Austria that Germany will definitely respect the Austrian status quo. The key to the mutual compromise between Germany and Italy lies in this. Then the 'Central European Group' advocated by the German Emperor Wilhelm II will probably be revived to a considerable extent." (Havas dispatch, 10th)

Heat Wave Sweeping Across the United States, Extending from the Midwest to the East Coast 50

Heatstroke Deaths Reach Over Two Hundred, Wildfire in Michigan National Forest

(New York) The heat wave in the Midwest is now extending to the East Coast. It is estimated that the number of cultivable fields in the United States suffering from drought has accounted for one-third of the total. The temperature in New York today reached 101 degrees, only one degree lower than the record. Due to the hot weather, the two suspension bridges on the Harlem River were twisted, so pedestrians had to detour. There was slight rain in several places across the country today. According to the Weather Bureau, there is no sign of cooling down for the time being. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(New York) The death toll from the heat wave across the United States has reached 245. Twelve postal workers collapsed from heatstroke while walking to Harrisburg. Temperatures in Nebraska and Pennsylvania rose to between 120 and 125 degrees. A wildfire broke out in the national forest of Michigan, and 500 residents are now trying to extinguish it. In Indiana, a man went mad from the heat and killed his wife and six children with an axe, shot and killed a fellow worker, and then shot himself to death. The heat wave in the Midwest has now extended to the East Coast. The Midwest has been unusually hot for days, and today is the eighth day. There is no sign of cooling down for the time being. (Reuters dispatch, 10th)

(Chicago) The sun is still raging in the drought-stricken areas of the American Midwest today. Although there are occasional showers, it is of no help. Meteorologists here announced, "There is still no change in the central states today," which has led to the death toll from heatstroke and drowning reaching 215. Effingham, Illinois, had the most rain last night, with 2.46 inches. Strange Lake in Minnesota, which is right in the center of the most severe disaster, also had 1.48 inches. Unfortunately, the rain came too late, and the wheat in the fields there has withered. There were also slight showers here, but officials estimate that 500,000 people spent the night on the beach last night to escape the heat. The temperature in Iowa is expected to reach 108 degrees. The Washington Farm Security Administration has announced that rural rehabilitation loans can be suspended for one year to help residents in the disaster area. (National News dispatch, 9th)

French Minister of Finance Delivers Speech, Financial Situation Improving 51

Appeals to Citizens to Purchase Short-Term Treasury Bills

Work Together to Help Economic Recovery

Central Bank Reduces Discount Rate Again, Gold Outflow Stopped

(Paris) Minister of Finance Valivoire delivered a radio address today, appealing to the rich and poor across the country to purchase "baby loans" in order to restore national finances. He also said that the Bank of France will discount these bonds without restriction, and the outflow of gold has now stopped. In the past two weeks, more than 500 million francs worth of gold has returned to the country. These bonds are available in two types, with face values ranging from 200 francs to 100,000 francs: one is a one-year term with a 4% interest rate, and the other is a six-month term with a 3.5% interest rate. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

(Paris) Minister of Finance Olivol recently delivered a radio address to the nation, explaining the financial situation of France, saying, "The government previously applied for the restoration of national confidence. The people of the country have listened to this application and have understood that national welfare can only rely on self-reliance. This is gratifying. Today, the financial situation has suddenly shown a resurgence. For example, the franc exchange rate has loosened, and the discount rate of the Bank of France, which was increased to 6% in May, has now been reduced to 3% after government consultation. As a result, the public bond market has also improved. For example, the term interest rate, which was as high as 7% on June 15, has now been reduced to 4.5%, and the market price of public bonds has risen from 65.35 francs to 69.90 francs (market price on July 8). The example is also that we should rationalize the credit system, protect the savings industry, and reduce taxes, so that the national credit will be fully restored. However, this matter is of great importance, and many technical talents are now dedicated to research. The Minister of Finance then described the short-term treasury bills that the government plans to issue (a total of 100 billion francs), saying that the face value of these treasury bills varies, some are 100,000 francs, some are 10,000 francs, some are 500 francs, and some are 250 francs. The intention is to enable people across the country, regardless of their wealth, to purchase them. The benefits enjoyed by those who purchase treasury bills are also different. The term is extremely short, and the principal can be repaid after six months. It can be requested from the bank at any time for discounting. There are two types of interest rates, 3.5% for the six-month term and 4% for the one-year term, both of which are paid in advance by the government. These treasury bills are scheduled to be issued tomorrow. If the people of the country can actively purchase them, the prices of various public bonds will inevitably increase, the foreign exchange rate will inevitably improve, and the interest rates on deposits and loans will also be reduced. As a result, the costs of agriculture, industry, and commerce will inevitably decrease. In short, the government's responsibilities are extremely arduous, and it hopes that the people of the country will work together to assist it. It should be known that assisting France is assisting the cause of peace. I would like to express my sincere gratitude to the people of the country. If we can show our spiritual strength to the world, we can ask all countries to work together to clear up the economic chaos, the economic and financial wars, and the tariff wars, which are enough to destroy a country's foundation and cause conflicts between countries. It is necessary to stop them as soon as possible." (Havas dispatch, 9th)

Current Situation in Abyssinia Under Italian Rule 52

Organizing Indigenous Troops to Suppress Bandits

Dividing the Entire Territory into Five Provinces

Creating a Force of Muslims to Resist the Abyssinian Race

Cairo A Reuters correspondent who recently arrived here from Addis Ababa, the capital of Abyssinia, with the Northern Italian Army, Mr. Holmes, claimed today that the interior of Abyssinia is full of bandits, and the lives of Europeans are quite dangerous. Many of them have lost everything they own. More than a dozen Germans who are doing business in Abyssinia are now planning to leave with their families. The Italian army is now suppressing the bandits, often killing many people and burning the huts where the natives live. However, the Italian authorities deeply believe that the most effective way to eliminate bandits is to recruit bandits into the army, reorganize them, give them generous salaries, and provide them with new rifles. This method is currently being carried out in and around the capital of Abyssinia. In the near future, it seems that a cavalry of natives will be formed. The Italian authorities have divided Abyssinia into five major provinces, each with administrative organs. Italians in the capital of Abyssinia all call this a well-organized product of Mussolini's own brain, which will be used as a guide for the long-term plan based on the old Roman principle of division. Military construction in each province is different. The Illyria province is considered to be completely pacified and does not require many troops. It is said that only one division will be stationed. The Imperial Advisory Committee has now been established in the capital of Abyssinia, coexisting with the Administrative Council. The Administrative Council is an administrative body, while the Imperial Advisory Committee is used to recruit Abyssinian dignitaries and give them generous salaries. In addition to providing consultation, they cannot speak on political affairs. The same system is used in the provincial governments, so that those who used to be generals and presidents who obey the new government are rewarded. The boundaries of each province are based on race and culture, so as to avoid conflicts with each other. Special attention will be paid to the areas where Somalis and Harar Muslims live. The purpose is to create a Muslim force to resist the great plan of Arabia. Therefore, they are trying their best to please the Muslims. In the capital of Abyssinia and other places, construction is underway to build mosques. (Reuters dispatch, 9th)

Bulgarian Cabinet Reshuffle Inevitable 56

Political Parties Request Restoration of Parliamentary System

Sofia – Rumors have repeatedly circulated here that a cabinet reshuffle to restore a parliamentary system of government is imminent. However, current conditions suggest it will be delayed somewhat. Following a petition to the King signed by sixty leaders of various political parties, requesting the restoration of the past liberal constitution, the military authorities, who are the real rulers of the country, were greatly alarmed to see these individuals forming a common front. They immediately exerted pressure on the government, resulting in a decision by the High Military Council earlier this month to prohibit party members, especially party leaders, from joining the cabinet. The parliamentary system of government was interrupted two years ago after the failed violent coup d'état by Colonel Velchev and his associates. Now, the entire nation believes that even if the government opposes its restoration, it can only delay it temporarily. An unprecedented unity of opinion among Bulgarian political parties regarding domestic policy is historically rare. As for foreign policy, they are divided into the "National Unity Front" and the "Democratic Strength Foundation" factions. The government has tried its best to persuade some party leaders to support its "new measures," but failed. The political parties are now demanding a swift cabinet reshuffle, with the inclusion of moderate elements to guarantee free elections. There are only two paths now: one is to form a government that enjoys public trust, and the other is to continue the "non-partisan" and "national unity cabinet" system. This system was established in May 1934 by Colonel Velchev, the "hidden hand of Bulgarian politics," but he was sentenced to life imprisonment for plotting sedition. The current cabinet, led by Prime Minister Kiosseivanov, maintains its so-called "new measures" and has done nothing to restore the much-needed national prosperity. According to its political opponents, the cabinet's only achievement has been to bring Velchev and his associates to justice. Therefore, apart from the army, it has few supporters. Although the cabinet reshuffle has been temporarily thwarted, it will eventually be realized sooner or later, thereby restoring the parliamentary system of government. (Reuters, 9th)

International Business Telegrams

Special Reuters Business Telegram, July 10th 61

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price – Today's price is 139 shillings, down one penny from yesterday.

London Silver Market – Spot prices rose 0.0625 today to 19 pence 75, futures rose 125 to 19 pence 8125. It is reported that China and continental Europe sold, while India bought. The market is quiet.

Mount Isa Silver – Stable today, the 13-month opening price was 45.20-45.40, due to the rise in London silver prices.

Exchange Rates

US-UK – The London foreign exchange market was quiet and mixed today. The price of the pound in US dollars fell slightly. The opening exchange rate between the pound and the US dollar was $5.01875, lower than yesterday's closing rate by $0.09375. It rebounded $0.0625 an hour later. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the price of the pound fell again to $5.018125, a net decrease of $0.15625 from yesterday's closing.

Securities

New York – The market opened strong this morning, with most securities rising uniformly, led by railway and oil stocks. Trading was very active in the first half-hour. Utility, railway, and steel stocks continued to rise. After a period of calmness, market prices surged, with railway and oil stocks performing the best, followed by copper, iron, and automobile stocks. Near noon, market prices rose from a few points to one pound two five each. The New York securities market prices are listed below.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton – Cotton prices surged today due to high speculation and temperatures in cotton-growing areas, prompting large-scale purchases by dealers and individuals. The October contract opened at 12.8, up twelve points from yesterday's close. It gradually rose in the morning, and near noon, the October contract price was 12.73, a net increase of twenty-seven points.

Liverpool Cotton – The American cotton futures market opened stable today, due to purchases by dealers and speculators. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the July contract was 71.13, up eight points from yesterday's close.

Chicago Wheat – The opening was stable, but trading became active due to reports of clear and dry weather in American and Canadian wheat areas, causing prices to rise. At noon, the September contract price was 107.875, a net increase of one and eight seven five points from yesterday's close. Coarse grains were strong due to reports of harvest degradation and continued dry weather. At noon, the September contract price was 82.50, up twelve and six two five points from yesterday's close.

Liverpool Wheat – The opening was stable today due to news of Australian wheat shipments benefiting the bulls. However, the upward trend was partially limited by a Canadian agricultural department report favoring the bears. Later, market prices rose again due to American weather telegrams. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the July contract price was six shillings six pence seven eight five, up two five points from yesterday's close.

Rubber

London – The market was stable today. At 1 PM in the afternoon, the trading price for the October-December contract was 7 pence 8125, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York – The market was stable today. Prices fluctuated narrowly in the morning. At noon, the July contract price remained unchanged at 1666, but it had briefly fallen two points when it opened. The New York commodity market prices are listed below.

Japanese Add Sixth Military District to Puppet Organization Today 62

Intention to Consolidate Control of Soviet East

Puppet Headquarters Now Located in Mudanjiang – Harbin Correspondence: To facilitate attacks on anti-Japanese forces, defend against Russia, and control puppet troops, the Japanese Kwantung Army, since July 1st of the year before last, ordered the reorganization of the Northeast Provinces Garrison Headquarters into five major military districts (excluding the puppet Hinggan Province). Over the years, the Japanese side has considered these organizations to have become increasingly substantial and consolidated. Now, in order to strengthen eastern Manchuria, cope with the Soviet border area, and facilitate control, it has been decided to expand the original Suining District Headquarters, which belongs to the Fourth Puppet Military District, to a higher level, relocate it to Mudanjiang, and designate it as the Sixth Puppet Military District Headquarters. It will control military affairs such as border defense and security against Russia in Dongning, Muling, Ning'an, Mishan, Hulin, and other places in the east. This matter has been actively prepared by the Japanese Kwantung Army, the Puppet Military Affairs Department, and various responsible parties below the Fourth Puppet Military District, and everything is ready. It will be officially established in Mudanjiang on July 1st of this year. The position of commander of the Sixth Puppet Military District Headquarters will be assumed by Han Hao Wang Dianzhong, the former commander of the Andong District Headquarters, who has already taken office in Mudanjiang. Many Japanese and puppet military officials attended the inauguration ceremony.

He Jian Arrives in Nanjing from Hunan 63

He Advocates Peace Regarding the Current Situation

Consolidate the Central Government and Complete National Policies

Nanjing Correspondence: He Jian, Chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government and Director-General of the Pacification Headquarters, arrived in Wuhan from Hunan this morning, as the Second Plenary Session is being held today (the 10th). He then boarded a plane to Nanjing, arriving at 1:30 PM this afternoon. Accompanying him were He Chengjun, Hu Zongnan, and others. When He and his party landed at the airport, over two hundred people, including Cheng Qian, Gu Zhutong, Zhang Fang, and representatives from various military and political institutions, were present to welcome them, creating a very warm atmosphere. Reporters noted that Hunan Province's position is of great importance given the recent military actions in Guangdong and Guangxi. When He Jian was previously urged by the Guangdong and Guangxi factions to take the lead in resisting Japan, he expressed the need to resist aggression under the overall national policy and telegraphed all parties advocating peace. Therefore, the situation has been eased. It can be seen that He plays a crucial role in the overall situation. Therefore, reporters visited He's residence in Shuizuogang. As He was busy with official matters, he sent Liu Huarui, a consultant to the Hunan Provincial Government and the Pacification Headquarters, to meet with them. The conversation was as follows: "Mr. He Yunqiao was very busy with government affairs in Hunan, so he flew here this morning to attend the Second Plenary Session and must return to Changsha soon. Last month, the Southwest factions urged Mr. He to lead the resistance against Japan, but he replied by telegram, explaining the necessity of peace and unity, advising against hasty actions, and simultaneously advocating this view to all parties. Therefore, although the troops of Guangdong and Guangxi have entered Hunan and troops are stationed in Hengyang, both sides are very calm. This is the earliest result of Mr. He's advocacy of peace and provides great help to the future of the country. When the Southwest factions launched military action, the troops in Hunan had shared weal and woe with Mr. He for many years. Moreover, Mr. He is kind and benevolent, so there is unity and harmony from top to bottom, which outsiders cannot fathom. Mr. He is a leader uniformly believed in and supported by the military and civilians in Hunan. He advocates consolidating the central government and completing the overall national policy. He is selfless and comes to Nanjing this time to fulfill his consistent advocacy of peace. When Mr. He is in Hunan, no matter how busy he is with government affairs, his daily life is regular, frugal, and simple, enjoying the same pleasures as the people, and he has no bad habits. He likes to read famous works from ancient and modern times, both Chinese and foreign, and especially likes to study the progress of international military, political, and cultural affairs for reference. His martial arts skills are excellent, and his spirit and physique are both sufficient. Recently, he designated Hengshan County as an experimental county, so that scholars can have the opportunity to develop their talents. He treats scholars with respect and approaches people with sincerity. Fortunately, all parties value Mr. He's personality and advocacy, so the situation has not deteriorated. Mr. He's duty is to protect the territory and secure the people, and he also advocates universal love, harmony, and peace internationally. Except when resistance against aggression is unavoidable, he does not want to easily start wars between nations. He believes that the cultures and knowledge of the world's nations are all mutually disseminated and have mutual influence and benefit, and the races are distinguished only because of differences in climate and environment, but in fact, the world is one family." (10th)

Yellow River in Shandong Province Continues to Rise 64

Dangerous Work Occurs at Liuyuan

River Affairs Bureau Preparing for Major Floods

Jinan Correspondence: The water level of the Yellow River in Gansu Province suddenly rose by more than two meters several days ago, and its momentum was fierce and flowing straight downstream. It has now flowed to the lower reaches, so the river level in Shandong Province has risen. On the 8th, the water level at Luokou was 29.36 meters, up 2.5 decimeters from the 7th, and about two meters below the highest recorded level. However, the water level at Lishengtun, upstream in Shandong Province, was 57.27 meters on the 8th, about one meter and two decimeters below the highest recorded level, and slightly lower than on the 7th. It is thought that the rising water from Gansu has already passed, and the water level at Luokou may not increase any further. According to the River Affairs Bureau, dangerous work occurred on the 7th at the Liuyuan embankment (opposite the Kangtun dangerous work) in the Puyang County section of the northern bank upstream in the province. Due to the fierce scouring of the river water, two sections of the embankment collapsed into the water. Fortunately, the soldiers and laborers in charge fought hard to protect it, and it was quickly stabilized. The River Affairs Bureau has reported the situation to the Provincial Government. The River Affairs Bureau is now preparing for the flood season, which begins on the 17th of this month. Based on past precedents, flood prevention committee members should be sent to various sections to assist in defense. It is also heard that Han Fuju, the Director of the River Affairs Bureau, is actively reorganizing the river works. However, he believes that there is no need for too many flood prevention committee members this time and has designated 24 people (compared to over 50 in previous years), changing their title to flood prevention officers. They will be summoned for instructions in the next few days and then assigned to various sections to serve. In addition, for the convenience of conscripting laborers and supervising work, Han plans to issue an order, based on past cases, to the magistrates of the 22 counties along the river, requiring them to move to the embankment to take charge. (8th)

Qingdao: Lawsuit After Minghua Bank Collapse 65

Zhang Gangbo Sentenced to Four Years in Prison

And Deprived of Civil Rights for Five Years

Qingdao Correspondence: Qingdao Minghua Bank collapsed last May. Most depositors believed that Zhang Gangbo, the bank manager, induced depositors with high interest rates, resulting in savings reaching a huge amount of more than one million yuan, and used the stored money for personal squandering, which was a deliberate fraud. If he is not severely punished, how can we warn the cunning and maintain the rights of creditors? Recently, depositors such as Ding Bingnan specially filed a lawsuit with the Qingdao District Court against Zhang Gangbo for fraud. The court has conducted several interrogations and sentenced Zhang Gangbo to four years in prison and deprived him of civil rights for five years. The judgment was delivered yesterday, and the original text is recorded below:

Judgment

Plaintiff Ding Bingnan, Plaintiff Liu Xunmin, Attorney Zhou Feng, Defendant Zhang Gangbo, 51 years old, residing at Minghua Bank, Zhongshan Road, Manager, Defendant Xiao Wentian, 59 years old, residing at Continental Bank, Zhongshan Road, Manager, Appointed Defense Attorney Zhang Zonggeng, Right Defendants, case numbers 735 and 913, 24th, due to a fraud case, the plaintiffs filed lawsuits one after another, and this court combined the judgments as follows:

Main Text

Zhang Gangbo continuously intended to illegally possess property for himself and induced others to hand over their belongings through fraud, and is sentenced to four years of imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for five years. Zhang Gangbo is not guilty of other charges. Xiao Wentian is not guilty.

Facts

Zhang Gangbo has been operating Minghua Bank for many years and has established head offices in Shanghai and branches in Qingdao, Tianjin, and other places. In recent years, due to the impact of the global economic recession, knowing that it was difficult to continue operating, he induced depositors with high interest rates in order to achieve his purpose of fraud. Many citizens of this city were deceived, resulting in savings reaching a huge amount of more than one million yuan. Minghua Bank went bankrupt on May 23rd of last year. After more than half a year, there was still no way to repay the depositors. Subsequently, the plaintiffs filed a lawsuit with the court alleging that the defendants committed fraud.

Reasons

The defendant Zhang Gangbo in this case has been operating Minghua Bank for many years. In recent years, knowing that the business was declining and could not continue to operate, he still induced depositors with high interest rates and absorbed as much savings as possible. On May 23rd of last year, he declared bankruptcy. Until this year, he has been unable to repay the depositors. The plaintiff Ding Bingnan is also a depositor who deposited 500 yuan in fixed deposits and 100 yuan in current deposits in Minghua Bank and was deceived by the defendant Zhang Gangbo. It was found that most of the citizens of this city who deposited money in Minghua Bank were vendors and laborers who used their hard-earned money to deposit in Minghua Bank for interest to prepare for emergencies. However, things did not go as they wished and were defrauded by the defendant Zhang Gangbo, causing many people's lives to be unsustainable. Therefore, the defendant's criminal circumstances are extremely serious and should be severely punished. As for the defendant Xiao Wentian, on May 22nd of last year, he lent 20,000 yuan to Minghua Bank in the name of Continental Bank, and Minghua Bank transferred the mortgage right of Liu Xunmin's real estate to Continental Bank. This situation was not only unanimously confessed by the defendants but was also confirmed by this court's verification of the account books submitted by the defendants, so the defendants Xiao Wentian's crime and the defendant Zhang Gangbo's part of the crime cannot be proven and should be declared innocent. Based on the above conclusions, in accordance with Article 291, Article 293, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, Article 339, Paragraph 1, Article 56, and Article 37, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text.

Bandits Very Active in Southern Fujian and Southwestern Guangdong 66

But Most Large Bands Have Been Incorporated

Small Bands Should Be Easily Suppressed

Xiamen Correspondence: The border area between Fujian and Guangdong has been relatively quiet in the past week. Except for a unit of the Guangdong Army at Sancengling on the border of Dabu advancing 15 li into the Xiayang Township in the Fifth District of Yongding, there have been no new movements. However, the remnants of the communists in western Fujian and the local bandits in southern Fujian are extremely active. According to the latest report, Zhang Changshui's force of more than 200 communists in Heping, Puyang, and Jingyi attacked and plundered Guande Town in the Fourth District of Zhangpu at around 9:00 PM one night. The town suffered losses of nearly 100,000 yuan, and five district officials and strong men, and nine male and female citizens were killed. Twenty firearms were seized. In the morning of the second day, the bandits kidnapped Chen Wenpin, the chief of the Fourth District, who was also killed shortly after. Qujiang Town in Nan'an County, Quanzhou Prefecture, was captured by more than 200 communists led by Zhang Dingsheng on the second day. A drill instructor surnamed Xu and three members of the Zhang family, father and sons, were killed. A female teacher at the Taxia Elementary School was kidnapped. One bandit was killed and seven were injured. In Houkengpu Town in Nan'an County, Quanzhou Prefecture, more than 30 bandits posing as incorporated militiamen entered the town and plundered on the third day. The town suffered losses of more than 20,000 yuan, and the owners of nine major stores, including Zhenyu Dried Fruit Store, were kidnapped. Chen Meixiong, a bandit leader in Cixiao Township, Xianyou, raised the banner of the "Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army" and captured Ancuohoufeng and other villages in the Second District on the seventh day, looting and killing two chiefs and one strong man. On the eighth day, local communists ambushed a bus on the Zhanglong Road between Shizhong and Hutou, causing the bus company to lose thousands of yuan. Countless other small bands are looting everywhere. The recent activity of communist bandits in western Fujian and local bandits in southern Fujian definitely has a background. Moreover, Zhang Kewu, who previously attacked Datian, has now been incorporated, with more than 800 people gathered awaiting inspection. They will be organized into a security regiment, with Zhang Kewu serving as the commander. Zhang Chengfu, Zhang Yifeng, and Tu Feifeng will serve as battalion commanders. Currently, there are still small bands of scattered bandits everywhere in various townships in Dehua and Yongchun, extorting money. However, since Zhang Kewu has been pacified, the center of the bandit situation has been lost. The bandit disasters in Yongchun, Dehua, Datian, Putian, Xianyou, and Taiyun should be easy to quell. Next is Anxi, where the bandit situation is very complicated. Lu Zhenshan has gathered various bands totaling 800 people, occupying the Second, Third, and Fourth Districts of Anxi. On the sixth day, Cheng Zaoling, the magistrate of Anxi County, personally went to Changkeng and arranged to meet with Lu in Taozhou, intending to recruit Lu's troops and organize them into the Anxi Anti-Communist Volunteer Corps, limited to 500 men. If this becomes a reality, Anxi can also be somewhat stabilized. In addition, there are Guo Zongzhan, Xing Hai, and others with over a hundred people each, but they will be easily subdued.

Gansu Provincial Government Prepares to Afforest Both Banks of the Main Stream of the Yellow River 67

Sends Fan Shuxin to Conduct Survey

Survey Period About Three Months

Lanzhou Correspondence: The afforestation project along the Yellow River in Gansu Province has had its afforestation steps and work procedures drafted by Fan Shuxin, the forestry instructor of the Provincial Government. The Provincial Government has also issued a clear order appointing Fan to conduct a survey along the river in accordance with the work procedures to prepare for the implementation of afforestation. It is learned that after receiving the order, Fan is actively preparing everything for surveying the actual conditions of both banks of the river. According to Fan, the Provincial Government has made the greatest determination to promote the realization of the afforestation project along the Yellow River in Gansu Province. Currently, due to economic difficulties, the scope of afforestation is limited to the main stream of the Yellow River, and other tributaries are temporarily difficult to implement. Therefore, the scope of my survey is also limited to both banks of the main stream. The survey route this time is approximately 900 li long, and the round trip is 2,000 li. If the departure date cannot be realized by the end of this month, it will definitely depart from Lanzhou at the beginning of next month, so as to complete the survey as soon as possible. Regarding the route to be taken during the survey, it is planned to start from Lan County, proceed westward along the south bank of the Yellow River, passing through Xincheng, Yongjing, and Linxia, to Jishiguan. This is the starting point of afforestation along the Yellow River in Gansu Province (the border between Gansu and Qinghai). Then, cross the river from there to the north bank, and then survey eastward along the north bank, passing through Hekou and other places to Jincheng Pass, cross the Yellow River Iron Bridge and return to Lanzhou. Report the survey details after passing, and then depart from Lanzhou again, still proceeding eastward along the south bank of the Yellow River, passing through Fangjiaquan, Jianluogou, Dashengou, Jingyuan, Dabao Village, to the Gansu-Ningxia border at Wofosi. This is the end point of afforestation along the Yellow River in Gansu Province. After crossing the river from there, proceed along the north bank of the Yellow River towards Lanzhou, passing through Wofosi, Lutang, Beigang, Honggou River, Jinkou, Shuifutang River, and other places, to Jincheng Pass, cross the bridge and return to Lanzhou. After arriving in Lanzhou, prepare a report on the survey results and submit it for approval as preparation for the implementation of afforestation. The survey period is scheduled for three months. During this period, the survey may be completed.

Zhejiang Province Plans to Mine Molybdenum Ore 68

Rare in the World

Worth Four Thousand Yuan Per Ton

Hangzhou Correspondence: Yongjia and Qingtian Counties in southern Zhejiang Province are famous for producing molybdenum ore, which is the most valuable and rare mineral in the world and is used to refine steel. It is coveted by foreigners. In the past, unscrupulous merchants have repeatedly used it to apply to the Provincial Government for trial mining. However, the competent department of the Construction Department believed that the mineral is a rare product in the world, worth 4,000 yuan per ton, and is deeply related to military affairs and national defense. Therefore, the matter was carefully considered and not approved. It is learned that the Provincial Government has decided to mine the mineral and has been approved by the Ministry of Industry to issue a license for the province to raise funds for development itself, so as to avoid it being acquired by others in the future. It is estimated that the project will be planned and started in the shortest possible time. (July 10th)

Songjiang County Magistrate Seizes Bandit Weapons 69

The training of the local leaders in this county began uniformly throughout the county on the 4th. In addition to assigning personnel to reside in each district for supervision, the County Magistrate Li has been inspecting each training ground district by district since the 8th, riding the Yun Jian steamer, accompanied by the Captain of the Water Patrol Team, Fei Gongxia. The local leaders were all conscientious, which was very satisfying. Yesterday, in Shanyang, it was reported that Xu Ayun, the remnant of the bandit leader Li Jinxiang who had been executed, was hiding in Shuike. County Magistrate Li and Captain Fei personally went to the address to search. However, the bandit Xu Ayun had already fled elsewhere. After interrogating his mother, she was ordered to hand over two bandit weapons, one being a six-inch Browning pistol, serial number 35356, and the other being a lotus pistol used by Li Jinxiang when he first became a bandit. The gun has been induced and still has a bullet inside. There was nothing else. They were immediately taken away. It is said that County Magistrate Li had received the report about these bandit weapons in advance, so he forced the bandit's mother to hand them over.

Suzhou: Man Commits Suicide by Lying on the Tracks 70

Outside Qimen, near the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway bridge, at 7:00 PM on the 9th, a middle-aged man wearing a gray silk long gown lingered. As the Shanghai-Changzhou train passed by, the man lay down on the tracks and committed suicide. He was crushed to death on the spot, his body and head separated, a tragic sight. The local bailiff found a suicide note beside his body and immediately reported it to the local prosecutor's office for verification. On the morning of the 10th, the office sent Prosecutor Lü and a forensic officer to verify. After confirming that he had been crushed to death, they instructed the local bailiff to prepare a coffin and collect the body, pending identification by relatives.

Candle Industry Labor Dispute 71

Because of the decline in business this spring, the candle industry in the Suzhou area has collectively reduced its scope of operations. After the Dragon Boat Festival, each store laid off as many as 52 workers, causing a sudden increase in unemployment and widespread panic. The labor union immediately requested relief from the Party and government authorities, demanding reinstatement to maintain livelihoods. However, the employers' trade association stated that the issue of reinstatement was out of the question and presented four rational points, requesting that the Party and government authorities convene a meeting to revise the labor-management agreement. The County Party Headquarters has ordered the trade association to quickly explain the reasons for the layoffs and will convene a meeting of representatives from both labor and management and the General Labor Union and Chamber of Commerce within days to mediate and achieve the goal of labor-management cooperation.

Changshu: Verdict in Filicide Case 72

Zhang Lu, a widow from Fusang, Shazhou, had an affair with Wang Maoquan, a farmer from the same village. This led to her eighteen-year-old biological son, Zhang Yuqing, being brutally murdered by her lover. Afterward, she not only failed to investigate but also helped bury the body to cover up the crime. Subsequently, the deceased's aunt discovered and reported the crime, leading to the arrest of the adulterous couple and their accomplices. Wang Maoquan confessed to beating Zhang Yuqing to death. The case was adjudicated yesterday at 11 a.m. Wang Maoquan was sentenced to death for murder. Zhang Lu was sentenced to two years and ten months in prison for jointly concealing evidence in a criminal case against another person (twice). Ji Kouhou was sentenced to one year for jointly burying the body. Pan Chuhou, also involved in burying the body, was given a reduced sentence of six months due to being a minor. Wang Maoquan, dissatisfied with the county court's verdict, immediately declared his intention to appeal in court.

Outbreak of Plague in the Urban Area 73

It has been extremely hot and humid here recently. On the 9th of this month, the maximum temperature reached 92.1 degrees, which is more than six degrees higher than on the same day last year. People are sweating profusely and complaining about the heat. All government agencies below the government level have stopped working in the afternoon. However, there have been reports of cholera. A soldier named Yang from the security brigade felt unwell at 10 a.m. on the 9th, experiencing dizziness. In less than three hours, he suddenly fainted and his limbs turned cold. After being sent to the county hospital, he was diagnosed with true cholera and soon died. At the same time, cases have also been reported in the Xiaodongmen area. The authorities are currently taking preventive measures.

Rice Prices Suddenly Soar 74

Over the past week, rice prices here have suddenly soared, reaching ten yuan and fifty or sixty cents per stone, an increase of about one yuan and fifty cents. The prices of other grains, such as wheat, have also generally increased, causing panic among the lower classes. According to people in the rice industry, it is normal for rice prices to rise during this lean season, but such a sudden increase is unusual. There are two main reasons for this:

Due to continuous rain, the farming season has arrived, and the supply of rice is scarce.

After speculators were unable to manipulate Shanghai's gold standard public bonds, they shifted their attention to rice and grain, deliberately disrupting the market and causing instability. This county has been affected by this situation.

Wuxi: Railway Bureau's Response to County Chamber of Commerce 75

Following the smuggling case at the local railway station, the County Chamber of Commerce sent an official letter to Huang Boqiao, the director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, requesting that he announce the details of the smuggling case to clarify the facts and protect the reputation of local businesses, as there were rumors circulating that were damaging to their reputation. After receiving the letter, Huang sent a telegram to the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that the case of railway station staff in Wuxi protecting smugglers occurred before March of this year. Upon receiving a confidential report, the bureau immediately sent loyal and capable personnel and entrusted the special-grade Party headquarters of the two railway lines to handle the matter. Special agents conducted a thorough investigation for several months and confirmed that the information was accurate. The relevant personnel have been punished and the matter has been reported to the Ministry of Railways for review. Until a response is received, it is not appropriate to make any announcements. The investigation into who was colluding with the smugglers does not fall under the bureau's discipline management, so no investigation will be conducted. The bureau has no knowledge of the points mentioned in the local newspapers and cannot respond.

Summer Suspension of Initiation into Abstinence 76

The County Anti-Smoking Committee held its sixth meeting yesterday, chaired by Li Tiping. The following resolutions were made:

The addition of 7,770 yuan to the county's 25th-year land tax revenue as funding for the anti-smoking center seems inconsistent with the original principle of using anti-smoking revenue for anti-smoking purposes. A request will be submitted to the provincial capital to ask the provincial government to allocate the funds from the anti-smoking revenue as originally planned and to publicize the anti-smoking revenue to the people of Suzhou to demonstrate credibility and emphasize anti-smoking policies.

The committee will work with the correctional institution to assist the government in improving sanitation in the correctional facilities for smoking offenders. Committee member Li will negotiate with the county government and the local court prosecutor's office to handle the matter.

The county government will be requested to investigate and, following past practice, suspend initiation into abstinence during the summer to avoid overcrowding and the spread of disease in the anti-smoking center.

The revenue and expenditure of the committee since its establishment will be audited by committee members Cheng Jingtang and Xu Chizi before being submitted to the province for reporting.

Jiashan: Wealthy Merchant Robbed in Train 77

Li Ruoyuan, a wealthy merchant from outside Jiashan County, runs the Mao Cheng Xie grain store and often speculates in Shanghai's gold market, making frequent and large profits. On the 7th, Li traveled to Shanghai for business, carrying 1,800 yuan in cash and 17,000 yuan in bank checks. While the train was passing through the Xinlonghua station, a fashionable young man sitting next to Li, taking advantage of Li's drowsiness, forcibly robbed him. As passengers were getting off the train, the young man fled. Military police on the train were informed and got off to pursue him. The incident has spread far and wide, causing widespread astonishment.

Pinghu: Husband Murder Case in Fish Pond 78

In Yuchi, a village near Jinshan in the northern part of this county, lived two brothers surnamed Pan. The younger brother, named Axiao, was naturally weak. He married a woman surnamed Yang. Yang had an affair with her husband's cousin, A'gen. The night before last, at the second watch (around 10 p.m.), Yang secretly arranged for A'gen to come to her house. While her husband was asleep, the two of them attacked him with knives, inflicting a total of eight wounds to his head, arms, chest, and abdomen. Axiao, covered in blood, fled to his brother's house and told him what had happened. Soon after, his intestines spilled out and he collapsed and died. After daybreak, his brother reported the crime to the authorities. Yang and the father of the murderer have been arrested. However, the murderer, A'gen, is still at large.

Ningbo: Discussions on Rebuilding the Xinjiang Bridge 79

Since the completion of the Ling Bridge in this port, discussions on rebuilding the Xinjiang Bridge have been actively underway. It is reported that the Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association held a meeting the other day and decided to reorganize the Shanghai and Ningbo preparatory offices. The Shanghai committee nominated 39 members, including Du Yuesheng and Yu Zuoting. The Ningbo committee nominated 11 members, including Wang Wenhan, Yu Zuochen, Chen Ruxin, Zhou Dalie, Jin Zhenxiang, Yu Runquan, Mao Jiasheng, Zhu Xuchang, Zhuo Baoting, Chen Baolin, and Yu Jimin. It is planned to raise 700,000 yuan for construction, initially by soliciting 350 founders, each contributing 2,000 yuan. The materials will be sourced domestically as a principle. Zhang Jiguang, Yu Zuoting, and Wang Gaosun are responsible for the design. It is said that after the Xinjiang Bridge is rebuilt, it will be renamed Zhongzheng Bridge. The Xiangxi Highway was flooded by torrential rains on the 6th, causing the road surface to become like a river, making it difficult for cars to travel and disrupting traffic. Although the weather cleared on the 8th, the water had not completely receded, making it difficult to restore the road to its original condition. It is expected that traffic will resume in a day or two. In addition, over 7,000 dried fish stacked by the Yushang Fish Market near the Wuliao Bridge were washed away by flash floods after the heavy rain, resulting in significant losses. Countless houses collapsed and people were injured, making it a truly devastating calamity.

Yao County Government Executes Two Bandits by Firing Squad 80

Zheng Quanyao, a resident of Fushou Township, Yuyao, was kidnapped by bandits on the night of September 7th of last year and murdered when the ransom attempt failed. His body was dumped in Fuzi Lake. After the case was reported, the county government ordered the police to arrest the main culprits, Sun Meizhang and Li Ahong. After clear confessions were obtained during interrogation, they were sentenced to death. On the 8th, an order was received to execute the two bandits by firing squad. The other accomplices, Weng Ahe and four others, were each sentenced to 15 years in prison and sent to jail.

Xiaoshan: Reasons for the Soaring Price of Grain 81

The grain produced in Xiaoshan County is only sufficient to supply the county for half a year. The rest must be imported from neighboring counties such as Zhuji and Shengxian. Therefore, every year during the summer lean season, the price of rice increases significantly. This year, the new grain from Zhuji has not yet been harvested, and the hoarders are unwilling to sell at a fair price. In addition, surplus grain from other counties is being transported to Shanghai, Qingdao, and other places to be sold at high prices. Therefore, the price of rice purchased by Xiaoshan from Hangzhou and the Huzhou region has increased significantly. As a result, the price of rice sold in stores has risen sharply since July 5th, with the price of ordinary rice also exceeding one yuan per dou. The poor are complaining, and life is becoming increasingly difficult.

Cotton Pests Discovered in Dongxiang 82

Recently, due to the hot weather, a type of cotton pest has been discovered in the sandy cotton fields of the Kanshan area in Dongxiang. These pests specifically eat cotton buds and young leaves, spreading over thousands of acres. Although the villagers have tried their best to catch them, they eat very quickly and cause significant damage. The County Pest Control Committee has received reports and has sent personnel to the countryside to find ways to prevent and control the pests. It is also reported that similar cotton pests have been discovered in the Xinlinzhou area, and the Township Farmers' Association has taken measures to catch them in order to eliminate the damage they cause.
